I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Signed-Releases check ignores .sigstore.json signatures produced by sigstore/gh-action-sigstore-python
**Describe the bug**
The `Signed-Releases` check currently checks for:
> ...the following filenames in the project's last five release assets: *.minisig, *.asc (pgp), *.sig, *.sign, *.sigstore, *.intoto.jsonl.

For Python packages, the easiest way to create sigstore signatures is with the [sigstore/gh-action-sigstore-python](https://github.com/sigstore/gh-action-sigstore-python) GitHub Action. The GitHub Action's implementation when signing blobs produces a `.sigstore.json` file.

Since `.sigstore.json` does not match any of the file patterns in the `Signed-Releases` check, Python projects using this GitHub Action show up as failing the check when they do have valid sigstore signatures for their releases.

**Reproduction steps**
Steps to reproduce the behavior:
1. Run `scorecard --repo https://github.com/mark-adams/python-test-groups`
2. Observe that the `Signed-Releases` check has a score of 0.
3. Visit https://github.com/mark-adams/pytest-test-groups/releases/tag/1.2.1 (the latest release)
4. Observe that `.sigstore.json` files are present for all *.tar.gz and *.whl artifacts.

**Expected behavior**
Since these sigstore signatures are produced with the official sigstore GitHub Action, I would expect that the `Signed-Releases` check should have a score of 8 since sigstore signatures are present for the artifacts in each release.


</pr_description>

    50	        findings, err := zrunner.Run(pRawResults, probes.SignedReleases)
    51	        if err != nil {
    52	                e := sce.WithMessage(sce.ErrScorecardInternal, err.Error())
    53	                return checker.CreateRuntimeErrorResult(CheckFuzzing, e)
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        // Return the score evaluation.
    57	        ret := evaluation.SignedReleases(CheckSignedReleases, findings, c.Dlogger)
    58	        ret.Findings = findings
    59	        return ret
    60	}
    61

    15	//nolint:stylecheck
    16	package releasesAreSigned
    17	
    18	import (
    19	        "embed"
    20	        "fmt"
    21	        "strings"
    22	
    23	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
    24	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/finding"
    25	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/checknames"
    26	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/probes"
    27	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/probes/internal/utils/uerror"
    28	)
    29	
    30	func init() {
    31	        probes.MustRegister(Probe, Run, []checknames.CheckName{checknames.SignedReleases})
    32	}
    33	
    34	//go:embed *.yml
    35	var fs embed.FS
    36	
    37	const (
    38	        Probe           = "releasesAreSigned"
    39	        ReleaseNameKey  = "releaseName"
    40	        AssetNameKey    = "assetName"
    41	        releaseLookBack = 5
    42	)
    43	
    44	var signatureExtensions = []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore"}
    45	
    46	func Run(raw *checker.RawResults) ([]finding.Finding, string, error) {
    47	        if raw == nil {
    48	                return nil, "", fmt.Errorf("%w: raw", uerror.ErrNil)
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        var findings []finding.Finding
    52	
    53	        releases := raw.SignedReleasesResults.Releases
    54	
    55	        totalReleases := 0
    56	        for releaseIndex, release := range releases {
    57	                if releaseIndex >= releaseLookBack {
    58	                        break
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                if len(release.Assets) == 0 {
    62	                        continue
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                totalReleases++
    66	                signed := false
    67	                for j := range release.Assets {
    68	                        asset := release.Assets[j]
    69	                        for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
    70	                                if !strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
    71	                                        continue
    72	                                }
    73	                                // Create True Finding
    74	                                // with file info
    75	                                loc := &finding.Location{
    76	                                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
    77	                                        Path: asset.URL,
    78	                                }
    79	                                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
    80	                                        fmt.Sprintf("signed release artifact: %s", asset.Name),
    81	                                        loc,
    82	                                        finding.OutcomeTrue)
    83	                                if err != nil {
    84	                                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
    85	                                }
    86	                                f.Values = map[string]string{
    87	                                        ReleaseNameKey: release.TagName,
    88	                                        AssetNameKey:   asset.Name,
    89	                                }
    90	                                findings = append(findings, *f)
    91	                                signed = true
    92	                                break
    93	                        }
    94	                        if signed {
    95	                                break
    96	                        }
    97	                }
    98	                if signed {
    99	                        continue
   100	                }
   101	
   102	                // Release is not signed
   103	                loc := &finding.Location{
   104	                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
   105	                        Path: release.URL,
   106	                }
   107	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   108	                        fmt.Sprintf("release artifact %s not signed", release.TagName),
   109	                        loc,
   110	                        finding.OutcomeFalse)
   111	                if err != nil {
   112	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   113	                }
   114	                f = f.WithValue(ReleaseNameKey, release.TagName)
   115	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if len(findings) == 0 {
   119	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   120	                        "no GitHub/GitLab releases found",
   121	                        nil,
   122	                        finding.OutcomeNotApplicable)
   123	                if err != nil {
   124	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   125	                }
   126	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   127	        }
   128	        return findings, Probe, nil
   129	}
   130

   236	func release(version string) clients.Release {
   237	        return clients.Release{
   238	                TagName:         version,
   239	                URL:             fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/test_artifact/releases/tag/%s", version),
   240	                TargetCommitish: "master",
   241	                Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
   242	                        {
   243	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_checksums.txt", version),
   244	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_checksums.txt", version, version),
   245	                        },
   246	                        {
   247	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_checksums.txt.sig", version),
   248	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_checksums.txt.sig", version, version),
   249	                        },
   250	                        {
   251	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_darwin_x86_64.tar.gz", version),
   252	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_darwin_x86_64.tar.gz", version, version),
   253	                        },
   254	                        {
   255	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_Linux_arm64.tar.gz", version),
   256	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_Linux_arm64.tar.gz", version, version),
   257	                        },
   258	                        {
   259	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_Linux_i386.tar.gz", version),
   260	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_Linux_i386.tar.gz", version, version),
   261	                        },

    15	id: releasesAreSigned

    17	short: Check that the projects GitHub and GitLab releases are signed.
    18	motivation: >
    19	  Signed releases allow consumers to verify their artifacts before consuming them.
    20	implementation: >
    21	  The implementation checks whether a signature file is present in release assets. The probe checks the last 5 releases on GitHub and GitLab.
    22	outcome:
    23	  - For each of the last 5 releases, the probe returns OutcomeTrue, if the release has a signature file in the release assets.
    24	  - For each of the last 5 releases, the probe returns OutcomeFalse, if the release does not have a signature file in the release assets.
    25	  - If the project has no releases, the probe returns OutcomeNotApplicable.

    29	  text:

package releasesAreSigned

import (
	"testing"

	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/clients"
	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/finding"
	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/probes/internal/utils/test"
)

func Test_SigstoreUpdate(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []struct {
		name     string
		raw      *checker.RawResults
		outcomes []finding.Outcome
	}{
		{
			name: "Has .sigstore.json file",
			raw: &checker.RawResults{
				SignedReleasesResults: checker.SignedReleasesData{
					Releases: []clients.Release{
						{
							TagName: "v1.2.1",
							Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
								{Name: "package.tar.gz"},
								{Name: "package.tar.gz.sigstore.json"},
							},
						},
					},
				},
			},
			outcomes: []finding.Outcome{
				finding.OutcomeTrue,
			},
		},
	}
	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			findings, _, err := Run(tt.raw)
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatalf("Run failed: %v", err)
			}
			test.AssertOutcomes(t, findings, tt.outcomes)
		})
	}
}

    34	                        c.Dlogger.Debug(&checker.LogMessage{Text: fmt.Sprintf("GetProjectPackageVersions: %v", err)})
    35	                }
    36	                return checker.SignedReleasesData{
    37	                        Releases: releases,
    38	                        Packages: pkgs,
    39	                }, nil
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        for _, v := range versions.Versions {
    43	                prov := checker.PackageProvenance{}
    44	
    45	                if len(v.SLSAProvenances) > 0 {
    46	                        prov = checker.PackageProvenance{
    47	                                Commit:     v.SLSAProvenances[0].Commit,
    48	                                IsVerified: v.SLSAProvenances[0].Verified,
    49	                        }
    50	                }
    51	
    52	                pkgs = append(pkgs, checker.ProjectPackage{
    53	                        System:     v.VersionKey.System,
    54	                        Name:       v.VersionKey.Name,
    55	                        Version:    v.VersionKey.Version,
    56	                        Provenance: prov,
    57	                })
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        return checker.SignedReleasesData{
    61	                Releases: releases,
    62	                Packages: pkgs,
    63	        }, nil
    64	}

    30	var errNoReleaseFound = errors.New("no release found")
    31	
    32	// SignedReleases applies the score policy for the Signed-Releases check.
    33	//
    34	//nolint:gocognit // surpressing for now
    35	func SignedReleases(name string,
    36	        findings []finding.Finding, dl checker.DetailLogger,
    37	) checker.CheckResult {
    38	        expectedProbes := []string{
    39	                releasesAreSigned.Probe,
    40	                releasesHaveProvenance.Probe,
    41	        }
    42	
    43	        if !finding.UniqueProbesEqual(findings, expectedProbes) {
    44	                e := sce.WithMessage(sce.ErrScorecardInternal, "invalid probe results")
    45	                return checker.CreateRuntimeErrorResult(name, e)
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        // keep track of releases which have provenance so we don't log about signatures
    49	        // on our second pass through below
    50	        hasProvenance := make(map[string]bool)
    51	
    52	        // Debug all releases and check for OutcomeNotApplicable
    53	        // All probes have OutcomeNotApplicable in case the project has no
    54	        // releases. Therefore, check for any finding with OutcomeNotApplicable.
    55	        loggedReleases := make([]string, 0)
    56	        for i := range findings {
    57	                f := &findings[i]
    58	
    59	                if f.Probe == releasesHaveVerifiedProvenance.Probe {
    60	                        continue
    61	                }
    62	
    63	                // Debug release name
    64	                if f.Outcome == finding.OutcomeNotApplicable {
    65	                        // Generic summary.
    66	                        return checker.CreateInconclusiveResult(name, "no releases found")
    67	                }
    68	                releaseName := getReleaseName(f)
    69	                if releaseName == "" {
    70	                        // Generic summary.
    71	                        return checker.CreateRuntimeErrorResult(name, errNoReleaseFound)
    72	                }
    73	
    74	                if !contains(loggedReleases, releaseName) {
    75	                        dl.Debug(&checker.LogMessage{
    76	                                Text: fmt.Sprintf("GitHub release found: %s", releaseName),
    77	                        })
    78	                        loggedReleases = append(loggedReleases, releaseName)
    79	                }
    80	
    81	                if f.Probe == releasesHaveProvenance.Probe && f.Outcome == finding.OutcomeTrue {
    82	                        hasProvenance[releaseName] = true
    83	                }
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        totalTrue := 0
    87	        releaseMap := make(map[string]int)
    88	        uniqueReleaseTags := make([]string, 0)
    89	
    90	        var logLevel checker.DetailType
    91	        for i := range findings {
    92	                f := &findings[i]
    93	
    94	                if f.Probe == releasesHaveVerifiedProvenance.Probe {
    95	                        continue
    96	                }
    97	
    98	                releaseName := getReleaseName(f)
    99	                if releaseName == "" {
   100	                        return checker.CreateRuntimeErrorResult(name, errNoReleaseFound)
   101	                }
   102	                if !contains(uniqueReleaseTags, releaseName) {
   103	                        uniqueReleaseTags = append(uniqueReleaseTags, releaseName)
   104	                }
   105	
   106	                switch f.Outcome {
   107	                case finding.OutcomeTrue:
   108	                        logLevel = checker.DetailInfo
   109	                        totalTrue++
   110	                        switch f.Probe {
   111	                        case releasesAreSigned.Probe:
   112	                                if _, ok := releaseMap[releaseName]; !ok {
   113	                                        releaseMap[releaseName] = 8
   114	                                }
   115	                        case releasesHaveProvenance.Probe:
   116	                                releaseMap[releaseName] = 10
   117	                        }
   118	                case finding.OutcomeFalse:
   119	                        logLevel = checker.DetailWarn
   120	                        if f.Probe == releasesAreSigned.Probe && hasProvenance[releaseName] {
   121	                                continue
   122	                        }
   123	                default:
   124	                        logLevel = checker.DetailDebug
   125	                }
   126	                checker.LogFinding(dl, f, logLevel)
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        if totalTrue == 0 {
   130	                return checker.CreateMinScoreResult(name, "Project has not signed or included provenance with any releases.")
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        totalReleases := len(uniqueReleaseTags)
   134	
   135	        // TODO, the evaluation code should be the one limiting to 5, not assuming the probes have done it already
   136	        // however there are some ordering issues to consider, so going with the easy way for now
   137	        if totalReleases > 5 {
   138	                err := sce.CreateInternal(sce.ErrScorecardInternal, "too many releases, please report this")
   139	                return checker.CreateRuntimeErrorResult(name, err)
   140	        }
   141	        if totalReleases == 0 {
   142	                // This should not happen in production, but it is useful to have
   143	                // for testing.
   144	                return checker.CreateInconclusiveResult(name, "no releases found")
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        score := 0
   148	        for _, s := range releaseMap {
   149	                score += s
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        score = int(math.Floor(float64(score) / float64(totalReleases)))
   153	        reason := fmt.Sprintf("%d out of the last %d releases have a total of %d signed artifacts.",
   154	                len(releaseMap), totalReleases, totalTrue)
   155	        return checker.CreateResultWithScore(name, reason, score)
   156	}
   157	
   158	func getReleaseName(f *finding.Finding) string {
   159	        var key string
   160	        // these keys should be the same, but might as handle situations when they're not
   161	        switch f.Probe {
   162	        case releasesAreSigned.Probe:
   163	                key = releasesAreSigned.ReleaseNameKey
   164	        case releasesHaveProvenance.Probe:
   165	                key = releasesHaveProvenance.ReleaseNameKey
   166	        }
   167	        return f.Values[key]
   168	}
   169	
   170	func contains(releases []string, release string) bool {
   171	        for _, r := range releases {
   172	                if r == release {
   173	                        return true
   174	                }
   175	        }
   176	        return false
   177	}

    16	package releasesAreSigned
    17	
    18	import (
    19	        "embed"
    20	        "fmt"
    21	        "strings"
    22	
    23	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
    24	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/finding"
    25	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/checknames"
    26	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/probes"
    27	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/probes/internal/utils/uerror"
    28	)
    29	
    30	func init() {
    31	        probes.MustRegister(Probe, Run, []checknames.CheckName{checknames.SignedReleases})
    32	}
    33	
    34	//go:embed *.yml
    35	var fs embed.FS
    36	
    37	const (
    38	        Probe           = "releasesAreSigned"
    39	        ReleaseNameKey  = "releaseName"
    40	        AssetNameKey    = "assetName"
    41	        releaseLookBack = 5
    42	)
    43	
    44	var signatureExtensions = []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
    45	
    46	func Run(raw *checker.RawResults) ([]finding.Finding, string, error) {
    47	        if raw == nil {
    48	                return nil, "", fmt.Errorf("%w: raw", uerror.ErrNil)
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        var findings []finding.Finding
    52	
    53	        releases := raw.SignedReleasesResults.Releases
    54	
    55	        totalReleases := 0
    56	        for releaseIndex, release := range releases {
    57	                if releaseIndex >= releaseLookBack {
    58	                        break
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                if len(release.Assets) == 0 {
    62	                        continue
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                totalReleases++
    66	                signed := false
    67	                for j := range release.Assets {
    68	                        asset := release.Assets[j]
    69	                        for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
    70	                                if !strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
    71	                                        continue
    72	                                }
    73	                                // Create True Finding
    74	                                // with file info
    75	                                loc := &finding.Location{
    76	                                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
    77	                                        Path: asset.URL,
    78	                                }
    79	                                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
    80	                                        fmt.Sprintf("signed release artifact: %s", asset.Name),
    81	                                        loc,
    82	                                        finding.OutcomeTrue)
    83	                                if err != nil {
    84	                                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
    85	                                }
    86	                                f.Values = map[string]string{
    87	                                        ReleaseNameKey: release.TagName,
    88	                                        AssetNameKey:   asset.Name,
    89	                                }
    90	                                findings = append(findings, *f)
    91	                                signed = true
    92	                                break
    93	                        }
    94	                        if signed {
    95	                                break
    96	                        }
    97	                }
    98	                if signed {
    99	                        continue
   100	                }
   101	
   102	                // Release is not signed
   103	                loc := &finding.Location{
   104	                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
   105	                        Path: release.URL,
   106	                }
   107	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   108	                        fmt.Sprintf("release artifact %s not signed", release.TagName),
   109	                        loc,
   110	                        finding.OutcomeFalse)
   111	                if err != nil {
   112	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   113	                }
   114	                f = f.WithValue(ReleaseNameKey, release.TagName)
   115	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if len(findings) == 0 {
   119	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   120	                        "no GitHub/GitLab releases found",
   121	                        nil,
   122	                        finding.OutcomeNotApplicable)
   123	                if err != nil {
   124	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   125	                }
   126	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   127	        }
   128	        return findings, Probe, nil
   129	}

     1	// Copyright 2023 OpenSSF Scorecard Authors
     2	//

    14	
    15	//nolint:stylecheck
    16	package releasesAreSigned
    17	
    18	import (
    19	        "embed"
    20	        "fmt"
    21	        "strings"
    22	
    23	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
    24	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/finding"
    25	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/checknames"
    26	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/probes"
    27	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/probes/internal/utils/uerror"
    28	)
    29	
    30	func init() {
    31	        probes.MustRegister(Probe, Run, []checknames.CheckName{checknames.SignedReleases})
    32	}
    33	
    34	//go:embed *.yml
    35	var fs embed.FS
    36	
    37	const (
    38	        Probe           = "releasesAreSigned"
    39	        ReleaseNameKey  = "releaseName"
    40	        AssetNameKey    = "assetName"
    41	        releaseLookBack = 5
    42	)
    43	
    44	var signatureExtensions = []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json", ".intoto.jsonl"}
    45	
    46	func Run(raw *checker.RawResults) ([]finding.Finding, string, error) {
    47	        if raw == nil {
    48	                return nil, "", fmt.Errorf("%w: raw", uerror.ErrNil)
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        var findings []finding.Finding
    52	
    53	        releases := raw.SignedReleasesResults.Releases
    54	
    55	        totalReleases := 0
    56	        for releaseIndex, release := range releases {
    57	                if releaseIndex >= releaseLookBack {
    58	                        break
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                if len(release.Assets) == 0 {
    62	                        continue
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                totalReleases++
    66	                signed := false
    67	                for j := range release.Assets {
    68	                        asset := release.Assets[j]
    69	                        for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
    70	                                if !strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
    71	                                        continue
    72	                                }
    73	                                // Create True Finding
    74	                                // with file info
    75	                                loc := &finding.Location{
    76	                                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
    77	                                        Path: asset.URL,
    78	                                }
    79	                                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
    80	                                        fmt.Sprintf("signed release artifact: %s", asset.Name),
    81	                                        loc,
    82	                                        finding.OutcomeTrue)
    83	                                if err != nil {
    84	                                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
    85	                                }
    86	                                f.Values = map[string]string{
    87	                                        ReleaseNameKey: release.TagName,
    88	                                        AssetNameKey:   asset.Name,
    89	                                }
    90	                                findings = append(findings, *f)
    91	                                signed = true
    92	                                break
    93	                        }
    94	                        if signed {
    95	                                break
    96	                        }
    97	                }
    98	                if signed {
    99	                        continue
   100	                }
   101	
   102	                // Release is not signed
   103	                loc := &finding.Location{
   104	                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
   105	                        Path: release.URL,
   106	                }
   107	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   108	                        fmt.Sprintf("release artifact %s not signed", release.TagName),
   109	                        loc,
   110	                        finding.OutcomeFalse)
   111	                if err != nil {
   112	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   113	                }
   114	                f = f.WithValue(ReleaseNameKey, release.TagName)
   115	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if len(findings) == 0 {
   119	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   120	                        "no GitHub/GitLab releases found",
   121	                        nil,
   122	                        finding.OutcomeNotApplicable)
   123	                if err != nil {
   124	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   125	                }
   126	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   127	        }
   128	        return findings, Probe, nil
   129	}
   130

    45	
    46	func Run(raw *checker.RawResults) ([]finding.Finding, string, error) {
    47	        if raw == nil {
    48	                return nil, "", fmt.Errorf("%w: raw", uerror.ErrNil)
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        var findings []finding.Finding
    52	
    53	        releases := raw.SignedReleasesResults.Releases
    54	
    55	        totalReleases := 0
    56	        for releaseIndex, release := range releases {
    57	                if releaseIndex >= releaseLookBack {
    58	                        break
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                if len(release.Assets) == 0 {
    62	                        continue
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                totalReleases++

    67	                for j := range release.Assets {

    72	                                }

   128	        return findings, Probe, nil

//nolint:stylecheck
package releasesAreSigned

import (
	"embed"
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/finding"
	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/checknames"
	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/probes"
	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/probes/internal/utils/uerror"
)

func init() {
	probes.MustRegister(Probe, Run, []checknames.CheckName{checknames.SignedReleases})
}

//go:embed *.yml
var fs embed.FS

const (
	Probe           = "releasesAreSigned"
	ReleaseNameKey  = "releaseName"
	AssetNameKey    = "assetName"
	releaseLookBack = 5
)

var signatureExtensions = []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json", ".intoto.jsonl"}

func Run(raw *checker.RawResults) ([]finding.Finding, string, error) {
	if raw == nil {
		return nil, "", fmt.Errorf("%w: raw", uerror.ErrNil)
	}

	var findings []finding.Finding

	releases := raw.SignedReleasesResults.Releases

	totalReleases := 0
	for releaseIndex, release := range releases {
		if releaseIndex >= releaseLookBack {
			break
		}

		if len(release.Assets) == 0 {
			continue
		}

		totalReleases++
		signed := false
		for j := range release.Assets {
			asset := release.Assets[j]
			for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
				if !strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
					continue
				}
				// Create True Finding
				// with file info
				loc := &finding.Location{
					Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
					Path: asset.URL,
				}
				f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
					fmt.Sprintf("signed release artifact: %s", asset.Name),
					loc,
					finding.OutcomeTrue)
				if err != nil {
					return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
				}
				f.Values = map[string]string{
					ReleaseNameKey: release.TagName,
					AssetNameKey:   asset.Name,
				}
				findings = append(findings, *f)
				signed = true
				break
			}
			if signed {
				break
			}
		}
		if signed {
			continue
		}

		// Release is not signed
		loc := &finding.Location{
			Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
			Path: release.URL,
		}
		f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
			fmt.Sprintf("release artifact %s not signed", release.TagName),
			loc,
			finding.OutcomeFalse)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
		}
		f = f.WithValue(ReleaseNameKey, release.TagName)
		findings = append(findings, *f)
	}

	if len(findings) == 0 {
		f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
			"no GitHub/GitLab releases found",
			nil,
			finding.OutcomeNotApplicable)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
		}
		findings = append(findings, *f)
	}
	return findings, Probe, nil
}

    16	package releasesAreSigned
    17	
    18	import (
    19	        "embed"
    20	        "fmt"
    21	        "strings"
    22	
    23	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
    24	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/finding"
    25	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/checknames"
    26	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/probes"
    27	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/probes/internal/utils/uerror"
    28	)
    29	
    30	func init() {
    31	        probes.MustRegister(Probe, Run, []checknames.CheckName{checknames.SignedReleases})
    32	}
    33	
    34	//go:embed *.yml
    35	var fs embed.FS
    36	
    37	const (
    38	        Probe           = "releasesAreSigned"
    39	        ReleaseNameKey  = "releaseName"
    40	        AssetNameKey    = "assetName"
    41	        releaseLookBack = 5
    42	)
    43	
    44	var signatureExtensions = []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json", ".intoto.jsonl"}
    45	
    46	func Run(raw *checker.RawResults) ([]finding.Finding, string, error) {
    47	        if raw == nil {
    48	                return nil, "", fmt.Errorf("%w: raw", uerror.ErrNil)
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        var findings []finding.Finding
    52	
    53	        releases := raw.SignedReleasesResults.Releases
    54	
    55	        totalReleases := 0
    56	        for releaseIndex, release := range releases {
    57	                if releaseIndex >= releaseLookBack {
    58	                        break
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                if len(release.Assets) == 0 {
    62	                        continue
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                totalReleases++
    66	                signed := false
    67	                for j := range release.Assets {
    68	                        asset := release.Assets[j]
    69	                        for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
    70	                                if !strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
    71	                                        continue
    72	                                }
    73	                                // Create True Finding
    74	                                // with file info
    75	                                loc := &finding.Location{
    76	                                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
    77	                                        Path: asset.URL,
    78	                                }
    79	                                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
    80	                                        fmt.Sprintf("signed release artifact: %s", asset.Name),
    81	                                        loc,
    82	                                        finding.OutcomeTrue)
    83	                                if err != nil {
    84	                                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
    85	                                }
    86	                                f.Values = map[string]string{
    87	                                        ReleaseNameKey: release.TagName,
    88	                                        AssetNameKey:   asset.Name,
    89	                                }
    90	                                findings = append(findings, *f)
    91	                                signed = true
    92	                                break
    93	                        }
    94	                        if signed {
    95	                                break
    96	                        }
    97	                }
    98	                if signed {
    99	                        continue
   100	                }
   101	
   102	                // Release is not signed
   103	                loc := &finding.Location{
   104	                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
   105	                        Path: release.URL,
   106	                }
   107	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   108	                        fmt.Sprintf("release artifact %s not signed", release.TagName),
   109	                        loc,
   110	                        finding.OutcomeFalse)
   111	                if err != nil {
   112	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   113	                }
   114	                f = f.WithValue(ReleaseNameKey, release.TagName)
   115	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if len(findings) == 0 {
   119	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   120	                        "no GitHub/GitLab releases found",
   121	                        nil,
   122	                        finding.OutcomeNotApplicable)
   123	                if err != nil {
   124	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   125	                }
   126	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   127	        }
   128	        return findings, Probe, nil
   129	}
   130

   208	                        outcomes: []finding.Outcome{
   209	                                finding.OutcomeTrue,
   210	                                finding.OutcomeTrue,
   211	                                finding.OutcomeTrue,
   212	                                finding.OutcomeTrue,
   213	                                finding.OutcomeTrue,
   214	                        },
   215	                },
   216	        }
   217	        for _, tt := range tests {
   218	                t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   219	                        t.Parallel()
   220	
   221	                        findings, s, err := Run(tt.raw)
   222	                        if !cmp.Equal(tt.err, err, cmpopts.EquateErrors()) {
   223	                                t.Errorf("mismatch (-want +got):\n%s", cmp.Diff(tt.err, err, cmpopts.EquateErrors()))
   224	                        }
   225	                        if err != nil {
   226	                                return
   227	                        }
   228	                        if diff := cmp.Diff(Probe, s); diff != "" {
   229	                                t.Errorf("mismatch (-want +got):\n%s", diff)
   230	                        }
   231	                        test.AssertOutcomes(t, findings, tt.outcomes)
   232	                })
   233	        }
   234	}

    23	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
    24	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/finding"
    25	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/checknames"
    26	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/probes"
    27	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/probes/internal/utils/uerror"
    28	)
    29	
    30	func init() {
    31	        probes.MustRegister(Probe, Run, []checknames.CheckName{checknames.SignedReleases})
    32	}
    33	
    34	//go:embed *.yml
    35	var fs embed.FS
    36	
    37	const (
    38	        Probe           = "releasesAreSigned"
    39	        ReleaseNameKey  = "releaseName"
    40	        AssetNameKey    = "assetName"
    41	        releaseLookBack = 5
    42	)
    43	
    44	var signatureExtensions = []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json", ".intoto.jsonl"}
    45	
    46	func Run(raw *checker.RawResults) ([]finding.Finding, string, error) {
    47	        if raw == nil {
    48	                return nil, "", fmt.Errorf("%w: raw", uerror.ErrNil)
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        var findings []finding.Finding
    52	
    53	        releases := raw.SignedReleasesResults.Releases
    54	
    55	        totalReleases := 0
    56	        for releaseIndex, release := range releases {
    57	                if releaseIndex >= releaseLookBack {
    58	                        break
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                if len(release.Assets) == 0 {
    62	                        continue
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                totalReleases++
    66	                signed := false
    67	                for j := range release.Assets {
    68	                        asset := release.Assets[j]
    69	                        for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
    70	                                if !strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
    71	                                        continue
    72	                                }
    73	                                // Create True Finding
    74	                                // with file info
    75	                                loc := &finding.Location{
    76	                                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
    77	                                        Path: asset.URL,
    78	                                }
    79	                                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
    80	                                        fmt.Sprintf("signed release artifact: %s", asset.Name),
    81	                                        loc,
    82	                                        finding.OutcomeTrue)
    83	                                if err != nil {
    84	                                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
    85	                                }
    86	                                f.Values = map[string]string{
    87	                                        ReleaseNameKey: release.TagName,
    88	                                        AssetNameKey:   asset.Name,
    89	                                }
    90	                                findings = append(findings, *f)
    91	                                signed = true
    92	                                break
    93	                        }
    94	                        if signed {
    95	                                break
    96	                        }
    97	                }
    98	                if signed {
    99	                        continue
   100	                }
   101	
   102	                // Release is not signed
   103	                loc := &finding.Location{
   104	                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
   105	                        Path: release.URL,
   106	                }
   107	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   108	                        fmt.Sprintf("release artifact %s not signed", release.TagName),
   109	                        loc,
   110	                        finding.OutcomeFalse)
   111	                if err != nil {
   112	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   113	                }
   114	                f = f.WithValue(ReleaseNameKey, release.TagName)
   115	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if len(findings) == 0 {
   119	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   120	                        "no GitHub/GitLab releases found",
   121	                        nil,
   122	                        finding.OutcomeNotApplicable)
   123	                if err != nil {
   124	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   125	                }
   126	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   127	        }
   128	        return findings, Probe, nil
   129	}
   130

   217	        for _, tt := range tests {
   218	                t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   219	                        t.Parallel()
   220	
   221	                        findings, s, err := Run(tt.raw)
   222	                        if !cmp.Equal(tt.err, err, cmpopts.EquateErrors()) {
   223	                                t.Errorf("mismatch (-want +got):\n%s", cmp.Diff(tt.err, err, cmpopts.EquateErrors()))
   224	                        }
   225	                        if err != nil {
   226	                                return
   227	                        }
   228	                        if diff := cmp.Diff(Probe, s); diff != "" {
   229	                                t.Errorf("mismatch (-want +got):\n%s", diff)
   230	                        }
   231	                        test.AssertOutcomes(t, findings, tt.outcomes)
   232	                })
   233	        }
   234	}

   236	func release(version string) clients.Release {
   237	        return clients.Release{
   238	                TagName:         version,
   239	                URL:             fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/test_artifact/releases/tag/%s", version),
   240	                TargetCommitish: "master",
   241	                Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
   242	                        {
   243	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_checksums.txt", version),
   244	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_checksums.txt", version, version),
   245	                        },
   246	                        {
   247	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_checksums.txt.sig", version),
   248	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_checksums.txt.sig", version, version),
   249	                        },
   250	                        {
   251	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_darwin_x86_64.tar.gz", version),
   252	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_darwin_x86_64.tar.gz", version, version),
   253	                        },
   254	                        {
   255	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_Linux_arm64.tar.gz", version),
   256	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_Linux_arm64.tar.gz", version, version),
   257	                        },
   258	                        {
   259	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_Linux_i386.tar.gz", version),
   260	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_Linux_i386.tar.gz", version, version),
   261	                        },
   262	                        {
